          "definition": "CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.try_match_client_requests(p_car_id uuid)\n RETURNS void\n LANGUAGE plpgsql\nAS $function$\ndeclare\n  v_car record;\nbegin\n  select *\n  into v_car\n  from public.cars\n  where id = p_car_id;\n\n  if not found then\n    return;\n  end if;\n\n  -- match bem simples: s√≥ PEDAIS (type='pedido') e que batam marca/modelo\n  update public.client_requests cr\n  set\n    matched_car_id = v_car.id,\n    matched_at     = now(),\n    match_score    = 100\n  where cr.type = 'pedido'\n    and (cr.matched_car_id is null)               -- ainda n√£o tinha match\n    and (\n          cr.brand is null\n          or lower(cr.brand) = lower(coalesce(v_car.brand,''))\n        )\n    and (\n          cr.model is null\n          or lower(cr.model) = lower(coalesce(v_car.model,''))\n        )\n    and (\n          cr.price_min is null\n          or (v_car.price is not null and v_car.price >= cr.price_min)\n        )\n    and (\n          cr.price_max is null\n          or (v_car.price is not null and v_car.price <= cr.price_max)\n        );\nend;\n$function$\n",
